# Baseball Build Roadmap вЂ” Two Tracks (now в†’ MLB All-Star break)

**Status:** living В· **Window:** now в†’ the **MLB All-Star break (~mid-July 2026)** В· **Scope: baseball only.**
## рџ“Њ CURRENT STATE & FORWARD ROADMAP вЂ” by vertical (synced 2026-07-01)
*Supersedes the 2026-06-21 header snapshot below (retained as history). Detailed per-story tables + the incident board are further down.*

**One-line state:** the Snowflakeв†’S3 decommission is **~90% done** (the serving-critical path is fully off Snowflake); the MLB betting-edge search is **exhaustively closed** (markets efficient everywhere) but **RE-OPENED on the model side** because the features were found buggy в†’ a 2-week pre-ASB clean-features shot is live; the product is **honest-analytics** (calibration + transparency + tools), not a tipping edge.

### рџЏ—пёЏ V1 вЂ” Lakehouse decommission (E11.1) В· ~95% done
- вњ… **Serving-critical path OFF Snowflake:** W1вЂ“W6 (marts) В· W7a/b (clusters + readers) В· **W8a/W8b (feature layer + serving aggregator)** В· W9 (signal stores) В· W12 (sensors). Predictions serve from the S3/DuckDB lakehouse.
- рџ”„ **W11 вЂ” ALL ingestion в†’ S3 (the finish tail):** вњ… **Tier A + B(umpire) + C(weather) + D(public-betting) ALL SHIPPED** (C+D each also landed a new HOURLY time-series в†’ BOTH E13.16 precursors [weatherв†’line, public-%в†’line] now live + accruing). вњ… **Tier E CUT OVER 2026-07-03/04** вЂ” serving/eval reads were already S3-native в†’ E was writer-flips + bug-fixes + decommissions: в­ђ team-total dedup fix in `mart_derivative_closes` (unblocks E13.14) В· derivative live-writer S3-native В· `parlay_api` FULLY decommissioned В· `batter_pitches` retired (SF `stg_batter_pitches` leaf disabled first, else it'd HALT the build) В· venues flip. вЏі **Gating step = the SHARED SF-DROP batch: once the morning `daily_ingestion_job` confirms A/B/C/D all mirror green в†’ flip `W11_RAW_WRITE_MODE` `bothв†’s3` ONCE + DROP the 4 tiers' SF raw together** (operator already set all to `both`). **вЏ­пёЏ REMAINING: W11-FG (2 FanGraphs residuals + INC-26) = LOW-PRI last tier.** рџЏЃ **3 W11-E deferred flips are OUT-OF-SCOPE follow-up (PM call, NOT sign-off blockers):** `monthly_schedule` (naive flip re-triggers INC-20 OOM + bridge does load-bearing retention), `player_profiles` (SF self-read for incremental bookkeeping), `odds_snapshots_historical` (static 2.6M backfill, ~0 ongoing value) в†’ they join the by-decision KEEP category as bridge-retirement cleanup (do opportunistically w/ the Delta rollout, or never).
- рџЏ›пёЏ **By-decision KEEP (minimal Snowflake вЂ” NOT loose ends):** Cortex `daily_model_predictions` + narratives + the stateful model-state tables (Elo, sequential posteriors, SCD-2). **W10/W13/W14 deliberately NOT done.**
- вЏ­пёЏ **THEN в†’ E11.22** (feature-serving INTEGRITY audit + INC-24 closeout + model-health-gate calibration) = the single verification pass that declares the decommission DONE.

### рџЏ›пёЏ V2 вЂ” Platform: Delta Lake + Polars + DuckDB (the multi-sport on-ramp)
- в­ђ **E11.20 вЂ” DELTA LAKE (on-path) + POLARS dataframe over DuckDB вЂ” COMMITTED; the next MAJOR workstream after the decommission ships.** WHY: the recurring incident classes (INC-19 type-drift, INC-20 OOM, binary-ts misread, silent feature corruption) are all symptoms of raw-Parquet having no ACID / schema-evolution / retention / time-travel в†’ Delta retires them STRUCTURALLY. Acute driver too: the 40+min daily job (run_w1_lakehouse full-rebuilds history every run) в†’ Delta MERGE-into-partition. вљ пёЏ model-I/O gotcha: sklearn expects pandas в†’ keep a Polarsв†’pandas boundary at predict; adopt Polars incrementally (hot paths first, not the ~180 training scripts big-bang).
- **E11.21 вЂ” daily_ingestion_job perf audit** (folds into E11.20 / the Delta MERGE; run after the pipeline settles).
- вњ… **E11.20a вЂ” the DELTA+POLARS SPIKE DONE 2026-07-02 в†’ VERDICT рџџў GO** (decision doc: `docs/e11_20a_delta_polars_spike.md`; harness `scripts/spikes/e11_20a_delta_poc.py`). Ran on a `mart_pitch_characteristics`-schema table (local, no prod/serving touch): all 4 wins demonstrated (schema-evolution add-col = INC-19 additive cure; MERGE-into-partition; compaction+vacuum = INC-20 cure; time-travel as-of); Polarsв†’pandas model boundary written up; Delta read via DuckDB `delta_scan` (on par with `read_parquet`) + `pl.scan_delta`. рџ”ґ **ROADMAP CORRECTION surfaced: DuckDB does NOT write Delta (1.5.3/1.5.4 `delta` ext is READ-ONLY вЂ” `COPY FORMAT delta` doesn't exist; it DOES write Iceberg). The Delta WRITE path = delta-rs (`deltalake`/`pl.write_delta`), a new box dep вЂ” the "writable from our DuckDB stack" rationale is delivered by delta-rs, not DuckDB itself.** Other gotchas: vacuum(retention=0) destroys time-travel (keep 168h); delta-rs 1.x API churn (pin it); SF-ext-over-Delta carries the W8a binary-ts risk (moot if no SF Delta read); instance-role S3 auth for delta-rs (AKID landmine in new dress). Feeds the E11.20 rollout AC (quantify the MERGE win at real box-scale history вЂ” the POC couldn't at 1.5M rows local).
- **Sequence: E11.20a SPIKE now (parallel) в†’ decommission finishes (W11-E + residuals) в†’ E11.22 в†’ E11.20 FULL rollout (informed by the spike + audit) (+E11.21).** The full rollout waits for a complete + integrity-verified lakehouse вЂ” don't Delta-convert a moving target. This layout is replicated Г—3 in multi-sport в†’ choose+convert ONCE now, before the fall scale-out.

### рџЋЇ V3 вЂ” Edge / model (the pre-ASB push В· HARD 2-week clock)
- **Market-side edge CLOSED:** H2H Г—5, main total, K-props (E5.4), 6 model nulls, derivatives (E13.13), cross-market RV (E13.14) вЂ” all efficient.
- вњ… **E1.11 DONE 2026-07-02 в†’ CLEAN, now-TRUSTWORTHY NULL. The "features were just buggy" excuse is GONE.** Found+fixed 3 REAL prod defects (F1 stale starter-form / в­ђ F2 umpire+odds blocks serving ALL-NULL since the S3 cutover / Defect-3 odds blackout вЂ” F2/Defect-3 likely RESOLVE INC-24) + deployed traded-player enrichment; the deflation-honest re-test on the CLEAN substrate = 0/5 configs ship on both priority surfaces (correctness was collinear w/ existing feats; traded flags orthogonal-but-inert). в­ђ shipped a durable FEATURE-BLOCK COVERAGE GUARD (partial E11.22). в‡’ **`best_alpha=0` is now trustworthy; the model-DISCRIMINATION edge (out-predict the line) is genuinely CLOSED on clean inputs.** The correctness fixes stay (right on their own merit); no champion retrain. **вњ… PHASE 1 DONE 2026-07-01 (Opus) вЂ” audit complete, CI-green.** Dossier `E1_11_feature_correctness_dossier.md`; findings escalated to PM as a bug `E1_11_BUG_feature_correctness.md`. **2 confirmed defects (production features not correct):** (1) **stale starter form** вЂ” calendar `*_7d/_30d` has NO max-staleness bound в†’ 100% of the 9.43% of starter-rows with `days_rest>15` carry a *populated* "7-day" window (Teheran 189-day-old 2020-LAA form on his 2021 DET debut); `days_rest` itself is CORRECT. FIX BUILT (start-indexed `sp_*_l3` + `starter_form_stale`/`long_layoff` in `feature_pregame_starter_features`, Teheran-validated) but NOT yet surfaced into the 700-col matrix (raw wiring + box `--w8b` rebuild deferred). (2) **DEAD-IN-PROD** вЂ” lakehouse cutover silently zeroed the ENTIRE umpire block + odds-metadata in served `LAKEHOUSE_EXT` (0 vs 26,115 rows in frozen Snowflake) = W11b-umpire/odds box cutover not switched on. **в›” Phase 3 re-test BLOCKED until both close (PM decision).** Traded-player: 104 in-season new-team starts since 2021, no `is_recently_acquired` flag в†’ Phase 2. **вњ… PHASE-1 DEFECTS ALL RESOLVED + PHASE 2 CODE-COMPLETE 2026-07-02 (Opus, CI-green; box `--w8b` pending):** F1 start-indexed form surfaced+verified in served store (Teheran `sp_k_pct_l3=0.1154`); F2 was a stale ext-DDL VALUE:-case mismatch в†’ fixed by regenerating the ext DDL (umpire+odds now 98вЂ“99% populated all years); + a LIVE odds-bridge-freeze incident (Defect 3, 07-01 blackout) fixed (pipeline `--w6-odds-current` after spine rebuild + durable `check_odds_coverage` guard). **Phase 2 (traded-player correctness, both a+b, batters incl.):** acquisition off `stg_statsapi_transactions` (в‰¤30d flag, leakage-safe) inlined into starter+lineup features в†’ `*_is_recently_acquired`/`days_on_team`/`starts_since_acquired`/`form_spans_team_change` + pitcher NEW-TEAM (same-team) `sp_*_l3_same_team` form + lineup `recently_acquired_count`/pct/min/avg_days; 22 cols surfaced in the raw matrix (10 ::double-pinned). Batter same-team ROLLING wOBA deferred (needs current-game team = a scoped follow-up). Validated on real data. **вњ… PHASE 3 PRE-REGISTERED + INSTRUMENT-READY 2026-07-02 (Opus, CI-green; operator lift-runs pending):** the deflation-honest re-test is LOCKED before any run вЂ” pre-registration `E1_11_phase3_preregistration.md` + config suites `phase3_configs/{champion,perside}_suite.json`. Instrument = E13.4 harness `incremental_lift_eval.py` extended with **suite mode** (`--config-json`): all 5 pre-registered configs score against the ONE shared base IN ONE RUN per target, so PBO ranks {base,c1..c5} and DSR deflates by N=5 (not 1/run вЂ” the В§0.5 'count every config' fix; one-candidate-per-run hides the multiple-testing burden). **5 configs (full-coverage only):** `f1_startform` (start-indexed `sp_*_l3` vs the stale calendar block), `f1_staleness` (form_stale/long_layoff/age flags to gate it), `traded_pitcher` (is_recently_acquired/form_spans_team_change/starts_since_acquired), `traded_lineup` (recently_acquired_count), `all_enriched` (union). **Conditional <50%-coverage cols EXCLUDED by design** (same_team form / days_on_team / lineup_minВ·avg_days / pct=count/9 collinear) вЂ” they'd trip the degenerate-coverage guard; their value is within-cohort (a separate stratified study IF the flags lift). Targets/run-order В§6: perside_runs(CRPS)в†’home_win(logloss)в†’total_runsВ·run_diff(MAE), one invocation each. GATE = lift>0 (pooled+non-cold) AND PBO<0.2 AND DSRв‰Ґ0.95 AND not-degenerate; a clean null is the deliverable, a SHIP additionally needs a champion retrain (promotion runbook) before serving. 5 new suite-loader tests, fast gate 940. **вњ… PHASE 3 RUN + VERDICT = CLEAN NULL 2026-07-03 (Opus) вЂ” E1.11 COMPLETE.** Results note `E1_11_phase3_results.md`; outputs `ablation_results/e1_11_phase3_{perside_runs,home_win}_lift.json`. On the corrected+enriched substrate (bp_eb 6/30вЂ“7/2 backfilled + umpire block recovered pre-run), **0 of 5 configs shipped on BOTH priority surfaces** (perside_runs CRPS PBO=0.510; home_win NLL PBO=0.642) вЂ” every config `PBO<0.2=False AND DSRв‰Ґ0.95=False`, all reads valid (coverage 98.6вЂ“100%, no degenerate). **Two mechanistic reads:** (1) the F1 start-form fix is **0.73вЂ“0.86 collinear** with the champion's existing calendar block (`k_pct_30d`/`bb_pct_14d`/`xwoba_against_14d`) в†’ a *correctness* win but ~80% redundant as a *predictor* (lift в‰¤0.2%, DSR в‰¤0.58) вЂ” **correctness в‰  new information**; (2) the traded-enrichment flags are genuinely orthogonal (max|corr| 0.07вЂ“0.18) but **inert-to-negative** (DSR 0.04вЂ“0.27) в†’ the trade-mispricing hypothesis is FALSE at population level. `total_runs`/`run_diff` (#3/#4) **skipped per В§6** (both priority targets nulled в†’ optional confirmations can't change the verdict; documented skip). **Nothing ships / no retrain triggered;** Phase-1 fixes + Phase-2 enrichment stay deployed on their own correctness merit. This is the trustworthy version of the "no edge" finding the audit gated вЂ” measured on corrected inputs, `best_alpha=0` holds. Follow-ups left open (documented): within-cohort conditional-col study (low prior given flags inert); `home_team_sequential_bullpen_xwoba` INC-25 backfill (out of scope).
- **E13.16 вЂ” line-movement MICROSTRUCTURE** (odds-as-price-series) + **weatherв†’line** (W11-C data) + **public-%в†’line / reverse-line-movement** (W11-D data). A DIFFERENT mechanism (timing/CLV, not prediction) = the most-plausible remaining edge; forward-CLV-honest (accrues via the hourly captures). **E13.15** in-game probe = lower-pri.
- рџ”’ Every re-test runs the PBO/DSR/FDR deflation gate вЂ” the clock must NOT manufacture a mirage.

## Track 1 вЂ” Model build  *(2 model sessions: A = validation/totals В· B = market/infra)*
Ordered; lane in brackets. **E1's go-live gate is now CLEARED (E1.1вЂ“E1.6 вњ… + PBO/DSR + purged-CV on record)** вЂ” E2вЂ“E5 can promote to live once each clears its gate (PBO<0.2 + DSR>0 + forward-CLV).
> **рџ—„пёЏ DATA-FIRST PRINCIPLE (operator 2026-06-18): get the data into the best possible state BEFORE any retrain / the v6 bake-off.** Order on the model track: leakage remediation (E1.7 вњ… + E1.8 вњ… + the Stuff+ de-leak) **+ serving parity (E12)** в†’ **then** E1.9 (bake-off + retrain). Rationale: if the serve path is skewed, the bake-off's CV doesn't predict *live* skill, so it'd crown a model leaning on features that are null at serve. Fix the data/serve first so v6 is selected for what's actually servable.
> **рџ’° ACTIVE PRINCIPLE (operator 2026-06-18): keep Snowflake spend at the MINIMUM until profitable.** Snowflake is ~60% of burn and growing 25% MoM pre-revenue, so **cost-opt is now active work, not parked** вЂ” the E11 wave (rows 2вЂ“3) leads Session B ahead of E5.0/E5.1. Migrate jobs onto the **same lean lakehouse (S3 + dbt-duckdb on Railway) the new sports use**; new/changed transforms default off-Snowflake where feasible (В§6); the **live serving path stays on Snowflake and moves last.**

- **INC-12 вњ… RESOLVED 2026-06-23 вЂ” and it was NOT a feed problem: the dbt chain was correct the whole time (player_transactions / feature_pregame_injury_status / mart_player_profile_identity all had Civale ACTIVE, `is_on_il=false`).** рџ”‘ ROOT CAUSE = a SERVING-READ non-determinism bug: `api_cache` accumulates multiple `is_permanent=True` rows (one per write date; the `ON CONFLICT` only updates the same-day row), and `pg.get_cache()` did `WHERE is_permanent=TRUE LIMIT 1` with **NO `ORDER BY`** в†’ PostgreSQL returned an arbitrary heap-order row в†’ for Civale, a PRE-activation blob carrying both `is_on_il=true` AND the 5/25-frozen game log. **The coupling hypothesis was RIGHT** (one stale blob в†’ both symptoms). **FIX (generic, closes the whole class): `ORDER BY updated_at DESC` on the permanent-blob read** (`app/backend/services/pg.py:80`) в†’ most-recently-written row always wins. - **INC-6 в†’ вњ… RESOLVED 2026-06-21.** Sunday `dbt_daily_build` red-failed в†’ predictions blocked. Root cause: a malformed StatsAPI bio row (**zero height**) hit `stg_statsapi_player_profiles` during the weekly full-refresh; two `accepted_range` tests (`height_inches`/`weight_lbs`) were default-ERROR severity в†’ one bad row exit-1'd the whole `build` and killed the prediction pipeline. **3 durable fixes shipped:** (1) **SQL coerce** out-of-range bio в†’ NULL in the model (`CASE WHEN вЂ¦ BETWEEN`; range test skips NULLs, downstream imputes); (2) **severity downgrade** both bio tests `error`в†’`warn` (a bad bio row can never block a build again); (3) **build-path split** in `daily_ingestion_ops.py` вЂ” build days now run `dbtf run` FIRST (gates the pipeline) then `dbtf test` in a NON-BLOCKING `try/except` (tests warn, never fail the op). **рџЋЃ Bonus CI/CD fix:** the dbt-runner had no GitHub wiring (needed a manual `railway up` after every dbt change вЂ” the gap that complicated this deploy) в†’ new `.github/workflows/deploy_dbt_runner.yml` auto-rebuilds+redeploys on any `main` push touching `dbt/**` or `services/dbt_runner/**`. Verified Sunday build GREEN; pytest 405/405 вњ…, `dbtf compile` 1761/1761 вњ…. **в†” Advanced E11.7:** fix #3 already applied the run-gates/test-non-blocking pattern to the DAILY path вЂ” E11.7's residual is the broader audit (sensor/cron paths + the documented HALT/WARN/ALERT contract + the errorв†’warn severity sweep across ALL models). `dbt_daily_build` runs `dbtf run` on weekdays but `dbtf build --full-refresh` (run + FULL test suite) on Sundays; today's Sunday build hit two **error-severity** `dbt_utils.accepted_range` tests on `stg_statsapi_player_profiles` (`height_inches` в€‰ 60вЂ“84, `weight_lbs` в€‰ 130вЂ“375 вЂ” a placeholder/zero or bad StatsAPI bio on a new player). Because tests gate a `build` and `dbt_daily_build` is upstream of sub-model signals + predict, **one bad bio row exit-1'd the whole Sunday rebuild + blocked predictions** вЂ” though bio only feeds clustering features that impute downstream (never serving-critical). **Immediate unblock:** re-trigger the runner with `run --full-refresh --target baseball_betting_and_fantasy` (models, no test gate). **Durable fix (E-fix prompt INC-6):** (1) coerce out-of-range/zero height & weight в†’ NULL in `stg_statsapi_player_profiles.sql` (range tests ignore NULLs; downstream imputes); (2) **stop peripheral data-quality tests gating the serving pipeline** вЂ” downgrade bio tests to `severity: warn` AND split the Sunday path so models always rebuild + tests run NON-BLOCKING (`run --full-refresh` then separate `test`/`--store-failures`). **рџ“Ћ Same lesson as the catchup-job + INC-5: a data-quality check should ALERT, not HALT predictions.**
- **INC-5 в†’ вњ… RESOLVED 2026-06-19 ~17:00 UTC.** `schedule_capture` Step 2 (the dbt staging rebuild via `trigger_dbt.py` в†’ E11.0 runner) had been **silently no-op'ing on every cron fire since deploy** вЂ” `DBT_RUNNER_URL` was set to an **empty string** on the service, and the script's missing-URL guard exited 0 with only a quiet `print()`, so the job looked successful while `stg_statsapi_lineups`/`_wide`/`stg_statsapi_probable_pitchers` stayed stale until the overnight build. **Fix:** set `DBT_RUNNER_URL=https://dbt-runner-production-8899.up.railway.app` on schedule-capture (via Railway MCP, auto-redeployed) + **hardened `trigger_dbt.py`** вЂ” the silent skip is now a loud `WARNING:` to stderr (flush) so a misconfig shows in log tails. **Verified:** 17:00 UTC trigger rebuilt all 3 staging models (4/4 success); intraday refresh fully operational. `trigger_dbt.py` вњ… committed/pushed 2026-06-19. **рџ“Ћ Lesson (shared with INC-3): dbt steps must fail/skip LOUDLY вЂ” a silent no-op hid a half-dead E11.4 cron for days.**
- **INC-4 в†’ вњ… RESOLVED 2026-06-19 ~16:52 UTC.** `schedule_capture` (E11.4 cron) crashed every fire on `Invalid account identifier вЂ¦ no dots or slashes` в†’ intraday statsapi schedule refresh was down. **Root cause: a TRAILING SPACE in `SNOWFLAKE_ACCOUNT`** (`IHUPICS-DP59975 `) on BOTH schedule-capture AND weather-capture (same paste) вЂ” the connector rejects spaces with the *same* "dots or slashes" message, which masked the diagnosis (the hidden-char hypothesis was right). **Fix:** corrected the Railway env to `IHUPICS-DP59975` (no space) on both services в†’ auto-redeployed SUCCESS in ~35s; manual trigger verified Snowflake connect + 401 games fetched/inserted + clean run. **Hardening shipped + вњ… COMMITTED/PUSHED 2026-06-19:** account-normalization (strip whitespace/scheme/path/`.snowflakecomputing.com` + loud warn) added to `get_snowflake_connection()` in ALL FOUR capture scripts вЂ” `ingest_statsapi.py`, `ingest_weather.py`, `derivative_odds_backfill.py`, `odds_api_ingestion.py` вЂ” so this paste class can't recur. вљ пёЏ Surfaced INC-5.
- **INC-3 в†’ вњ… RESOLVED 2026-06-19 (E11.0c).** Original symptom: `sensor_ops._run_dbt` was a third, un-migrated copy that shelled `dbtf` locally (no `DBT_RUNNER_URL` check), so `statcast_catchup` ran the heavy `stg_batter_pitches+` subtree in-process on metered Dagster + hung ~1 hr. **Fixed:** consolidated to a shared `pipeline/ops/_dbt_exec.py` and sensor_ops now **delegates to the runner** (confirmed вЂ” it hits the runner, gets 409s, polls to completion). **Bonus fix discovered en route:** the dbt-runner is **single-tenant (HTTP 409 on concurrent `/run`)** and the client never backed off вЂ” `_run_dbt_remote` called `raise_for_status()` so a 409 became an HTTPError that Dagster's `RetryPolicy` burned through в†’ job failed. Now on 409 the op raises **`RetryRequested(max_retries=40, seconds_to_wait=30)`** в†’ Dagster **releases the compute slot during the wait** (no billed idle; iteration-1's sleep-loop had held the slot ~13 min billed) and re-executes when the runner frees up (20-min budget). 19/19 tests green (incl. the `test_dbt_runner.py` assert that E1.9 flagged вЂ” fixed here, not E1.9). Files: `_dbt_exec.py`, `test_dbt_runner.py`. **рџ“Ћ Note вЂ” single-tenant runner is now a shared chokepoint:** statcast_catchup + daily_ingestion + odds rebuilds + schedule_capture all route to ONE runner; 409-serialization is handled gracefully but if heavy dbt runs pile up this is a future capacity item (queue or 2nd instance) вЂ” fine at beta scale. **в†” E11.0b overlap:** the 409-wait is now compute-free (E11.0b philosophy), but the in-run `/status` blocking-poll still meters during the actual dbt run вЂ” that residual is still E11.0b's job.

- **INC-2 в†’ вњ… FULLY RESOLVED 2026-06-21 (E11.6 shipped) вЂ” last open incident; board now CLEAR.** Decommissioned dead Parlay from the pipeline + dbt: removed the 3 Parlay ingestion ops (daily job head rewired to `ingest_action_network`), gutted `pregame_odds_snapshot`в†’no-op stub + removed dead `lineup_odds_snapshot`; cleaned the 3 odds marts (`mart_odds_outcomes` parlay union removed, **historical Parlay rows kept as cold archive**; `mart_game_odds_bridge` parlay CTEs gone, `parlay_api_event_id` preserved as `NULL` for downstream schema compat; `mart_odds_line_movement` dropped the placeholder-time workaround CTEs, now uses real Odds-API `commence_time`); removed the 4 Parlay freshness alert configs (`sources.yml` source block retained so `stg_parlayapi_*` still compile for cold-archive). **Value-preserving вЂ” Snowflake parity вњ…** (`parlay_api_event_id=0` all bridge rows, no parlay in line-movement, cold archive intact). CI: pytest 405/1, `dbtf compile` 1761/1761 вњ…. **вЏ­пёЏ Operator follow-on cleanups (PM-approved, low-priority, non-blocking) в†’ `E11.6b`:** (1) **remove** the 17 dormant `odds_snapshot_schedules` in `intraday_schedules.py` (Parlay is permanent-off, the "manual failover" is dead вЂ” APPROVED); (2) **keep** `stg_parlayapi_*` staging (cold archive вЂ” agreed); (3) **remove** the now-no-op `pregame_snapshot_job` from `sensor_jobs.py`/`jobs/__init__.py` (APPROVED, when convenient). _(The `deploy_dbt_runner.yml` auto-deploy workflow also confirmed shipped here вЂ” already credited under INC-6.)_
- **INC-2 (original audit note, 2026-06-19): NOT a live-data-integrity incident.** Parlay API is permanently off (operator-confirmed). **Lineage audit verdict: the live serving path was ALREADY repointed off Parlay в†’ The Odds API on 2026-06-16 (Story 12.3.7/A2.18)**, *before* the permanent-decommission call. Live `feature_pregame_edge_market`/`feature_pregame_odds_features` get 2026 odds from The Odds API в†’ **no stale-odds risk to live picks.** **Also corrected:** the E11.5 session's "E2.0b moot" was WRONG вЂ” E2.0b runs on The Odds API (`oddsapi`), unaffected. **в†’ Converted to a cleanup story (E11.6, Track 1 Session B):** (1) remove the still-present `parlay_api_ingestion.py` calls in `daily_ingestion_ops.py` (L232/237/242) + `sensor_ops.py` (L248вЂ“273) вЂ” with Parlay dead they fail/hang each run (bounded by the 600s ceiling: noisy, non-blocking); (2) prune the dead `stg_parlayapi_*` branch from `mart_odds_outcomes`/`mart_game_odds_bridge`/`mart_odds_line_movement`; (3) drop the 4 warn-only `parlayapi` freshness blocks + the `parlayapi` source once tables are retired. Low priority; do AFTER the E11.5/T2 deploy + W1.
- **INC-1 (P1) вЂ” weekly `train_bayesian_meta_model_op` failed (h2h + totals): вњ… RESOLVED 2026-06-18.** Root cause: the Dagster **runtime image was missing `pymc` + `h5py`** (both in `pyproject.toml`/dev env but never in the Dockerfile; E9.2 had added arviz/h5netcdf for the serve-side but missed the training deps). **Fix:** added `pymc` + `h5py` to the Dockerfile pip block + a **build-time Bayesian-dep import smoke-check `RUN`** (the prevention we flagged вЂ” fails the image build loudly if a dep is absent). **Sessions:** Session A = per-side totals + bullpen + the slim re-promote; Session B = data ingestion (E2.0, E5.0/E5.1). **E5 pricing (E5.2+)** is the props edge test вЂ” starts once ingestion lands.

**Deprioritized by the E1 audit:** **E6.1/E6.3 generic feature work** вЂ” E1.3 delivered the redundancy finding (the slim contracts), and the audit concluded **more features в‰  edge.** ~~The one feature-investment direction that survives is bullpen~~ вЂ” **CORRECTED 2026-06-18 (E2.1b):** the bullpen "signal" was largely a **leak** (`bp_eb_xwoba` peeks at `outs_in_game`); the only real pre-game bullpen signal is **data-depth (`coverage_pct`/`uncertainty`), and it's modest.** There is **no "deepen the bullpen model" investment** to chase вЂ” the actionable item is the **de-leak correctness fix (E1.7)**, not more bullpen modeling.

**Realistic by the break:** **the production de-leak (E1.7)** landed + champions re-evaluated honestly; **totals distribution calibrated (E2.1вЂ“E2.3)** + derivative backfill (E2.0) staged; **prop data ingested (E5.0/E5.1)**. The betting-edge hope rests on **totals-derivatives + props** вЂ” H2H straight-bet edge is closed, and the apparent bullpen signal turned out to be a leak (see *Decisions*).

## Decisions & kills (on record)
- **рџ”¬ MODELING BAKE-OFF DISCIPLINE вЂ” STANDING STANDARD (operator 2026-06-24, after the E5.2 lapse). Codified: guide В§0.5 + CLAUDE.md conventions.** Any story that BUILDS or SELECTS a predictive model runs a **bake-off, not a single architecture**: pre-register в‰Ґ3 candidate model classes (a prescribed structure is ONE candidate, always with a direct-learned foil), Optuna-tune each, feature-ablate, pick on the metric under purged/embargoed CV PER TIER, guard the search with PBO<0.2/DSR>0. **A single architecture missing its gate is NOT a trustworthy null** вЂ” that's earned only after the whole candidate set, tuned + ablated, fails (with the mechanism named). Exemplar = **E1.9 v6** (6 learner classes в†’ Optuna в†’ gate; glm/ngboost WON, weren't assumed). Exceptions: pure registration/backfill (E2.5), cheap sub-model re-eval (E13.3), explicit harness/eval (E13.4). Prompts injected: **E5.2, E2.4, E2.6, E13.9**. **вњ… VINDICATED 2026-06-25 by E5.2:** the mandated bake-off (9 configs, PBO=0.0) found the LEARNED `poisson_glm_k` beats the originally-shipped hand-built compound on CRPS (1.236 vs 1.270) AND ECE (0.010 vs 0.035) вЂ” i.e. the single-architecture first pass would have served a measurably worse-calibrated model. The standard caught a real quality gap, not a hypothetical one.
  - **вљ пёЏ REVISIT AUDIT (completed model stories vs the new standard, 2026-06-24):**
    - **рџ”ґ E2.1 (per-side count model) вЂ” REVISIT (HIGH).** Built as a SINGLE architecture: `LightGBM Poisson mean + MLE NegBin r`, compared only vs a Poisson baseline вЂ” no learner bake-off, no Optuna, no learned-count foils (XGBoost/CatBoost/NGBoost-native-count, GLM). **It's LOAD-BEARING** (every totals model convolves it: E2.3/E2.4/E2.6), and E2.3's run-diff PIT near-miss + the ~24% dispersion gap trace to the per-side MARGINAL quality в†’ a proper per-side mean bake-off + Optuna could tighten calibration materially. **Highest-value revisit on the board в†’ written up as E2.1-r (prompt READY in `story_prompts.md`, 2026-06-24): в‰Ґ5-candidate bake-off (LightGBM/XGBoost/CatBoost/NGBoost-native/GLM Г— 2-step-vs-joint dispersion) в†’ Optuna в†’ picked on the CONVOLVED-total calib, PBO/DSR-guarded.** вљ пёЏ E2.1-r is UPSTREAM of E2.5/E2.6 вЂ” ideally run BEFORE them, else those may need a re-run if the marginals change.
    - **рџџЎ E13.2 Phase 1 (PA-outcome model) вЂ” REVISIT (CONDITIONAL, MED-LOW).** Null was declared on essentially ONE learner (LightGBM multiclass), no Optuna/CatBoost/NGBoost. BUT the null mechanism (86% batterГ—pitcher IDENTITY priors в†’ log5 captures by construction; per-class ECE 0.0026) is **architecture-robust** вЂ” a different GBM is unlikely to beat log5 if the signal is identity. So: already PARKED; **IF reopened (E13.10 zone-matchup trigger), add the learner bake-off + Optuna before any FINAL null** вЂ” but don't expect it to overturn.
    - **рџџў E1.9 v6 вЂ” COMPLIANT (no revisit):** full 6-learner bake-off + Optuna + per-tier purged CV + PBO/DSR. The exemplar.
    - **рџџў E13.6 (calibration) вЂ” COMPLIANT-enough:** TemperatureCalibrator was a REASONED Temperature-vs-Platt choice (contamination в†’ robust 1-param), documented вЂ” a deliberate candidate comparison, not a blind single-pick. No revisit.
    - **рџџў E3.1 (line-movement regression / "predict-the-move") вЂ” NO REVISIT (operator-flagged 2026-06-25; market-bound null, not architecture-bound).** Yes, the first pass was a single architecture, BUT вЂ” unlike E2.1, whose limiter is MODEL quality вЂ” E3.1's limiter is **MARKET EFFICIENCY**, which no bake-off can overcome. The "no cashable CLV/H2H edge" verdict is the program's most-corroborated null, from 4 independent angles: **E4.3** (the deeper version of the same CLV idea вЂ” found a REAL monotone CLV gradient but ~0.5вЂ“0.9pp vs ~4% vig = structurally SUB-VIG), **E1.9** (full 6-learner bake-off + Optuna в†’ thin), **E13.1** (distinct market-anchored-residual architecture в†’ strictly worse), and **E13.8** (empirical benchmark: H2H closes ~0.245 Brier, no headroom вЂ” the price is efficient). A bake-off would hit E13.8's efficiency wall + E4.3's sub-vig ceiling = mechanism-robust (like E13.2 but empirically pinned). Reopening also contradicts the deliberate pivot to derivatives/props. **If the appetite to retest "find CLV edge with optimal features" is ever real, the DISCIPLINED SUCCESSOR is E13.9 (selective best-bet вЂ” pre-registered, PBO/DSR, abstention, aimed at the SOFT markets), NOT an E3.1 redo.** (Same applies to E4/E13.1 вЂ” all market-bound, all corroborated; no revisit.)
- **E1 вњ… COMPLETE (2026-06-18)** вЂ” full audit arc built + validated (E1.1вЂ“E1.6); PBO/DSR + purged-CV on record в†’ **the go-live gate is set.** Findings: **(1)** ~~no leakage in any champion~~ в†’ **PARTIALLY OVERTURNED (see E2.1b): a within-game leak *was* present and purged CV missed it** (it guards temporal/cross-fold leakage, not a feature peeking at its own row); **(2) massively over-parameterized** вЂ” ~370 feats в†’ **14/31/19** with no loss в†’ re-promote on the slim contracts (**but re-derive post-de-leak вЂ” finding #3 contaminated the ranking**); **(3)** ~~bullpen EB dominates every target в†’ clearest signal-investment direction~~ в†’ **вќЊ RETRACTED 2026-06-18: that #1/#2 rank was leak-inflated** (`bp_eb_xwoba` weights by `outs_in_game`); de-leaked, it collapses to noise (0% retained). The real bullpen signal is **data-depth (coverage/uncertainty), modest**; **(4) history extension (E1.6) is a wash** в†’ don't extend history. **Revised conclusion: the edge is the E2 per-side-totals *architecture* (honest distribution/derivatives), NOT a bullpen signal; the most valuable action E1 surfaced is the de-leak (E1.7).**
- **E2.1b вњ… COMPLETE вЂ” "gate FAIL by design" (2026-06-18)** вЂ” bullpen deepening cannot beat the incumbent because the incumbent is a **within-game leak**, proven 3 ways (leak-signature: de-leaked equal-weight 2.4582 в‰€ v3 2.4571, both lose to leaky-static 2.4303 by an identical ~0.027; source `eb_bullpen_team_posteriors.sql:33`; MDA collapse #1/#2 в†’ noise, 0% retained). **Blast radius: the leaky column is in the live home_win/run_diff/total_runs training matrices в†’ a named mechanism for the offlineв†’live skill collapse (corr 0.42 в†’ 0.001), previously filed under "serving skew."** `bullpen_v3` not promoted (no real lift). Experiment B (per-relieverГ—handedness EB) explicitly **not** pursued (zero headroom). в†’ **action: E1.7 de-leak.** Full detail: `E2_1b_HANDOFF.md`.
- **E1.7 вњ… SHIPPED + VALIDATED (2026-06-18)** вЂ” production de-leak (Path A pure-dbt, equal-weight). **Two leaks fixed:** the `outs_in_game` weight **and** the appeared-in-game roster (which made `bp_eb_xwoba` **null for the scheduled slate at serve time** вЂ” the serving-null half of the 0.42в†’0.001 collapse, now mechanistically named). **Serving-null fixed: 37/37 scheduled games populate (was 0); 96.9вЂ“98.9% historical coverage.** Parity вњ… (Jaccard 1.0, corr 0.962). **MDA collapse confirmed on ALL 3 targets** вЂ” the leak inflated bullpen on every head, not just totals; `coverage_pct` (data depth) is the real, modest signal that rises to #1/#2. **рџџў Encouraging reveal:** de-leaking the H2H contracts surfaced **`elo_diff` + `pythagorean_win_exp_diff`** as real team-strength signals the leaky bullpen rank had been *masking* вЂ” i.e. removing the leak didn't just subtract, it uncovered sensible fundamentals. Slim contracts re-derived **INTERIM** (re-derive after E1.8); retrains (step E) gated post-E1.8. Detail: `E1_7_HANDOFF.md`.
- **E1.8 вњ… COMPLETE (2026-06-18) вЂ” leakage sweep verdict: the bullpen leak was the STANDOUT, not an iceberg.** Swept every signal-bearing + slim-contract feature Г— 3 targets (construction audit + serving-parity + leak-signature A/B, traced to dbt SQL). Post-E1.7 the construction surface is **essentially leak-free** вЂ” exactly **2 residual leaks:** рџџҐ FanGraphs **Stuff+/arsenal = leaky-season-to-date** (no `< game_date` guard; importance collapsed ~88% de-leaked but tiny accuracy impact; it sat in the totals slim contract в†’ de-leaked, held for E1.9) + рџџЁ catcher framing (noise, no contract, staged). Everything else as-of-safe (bullpen E1.7 fix confirmed live; sequential posteriors safe via consumer-enforced `prior_mu`/strict-`<`; H2H + run_diff slim contracts **fully clean**). **рџЋЇ Gap attribution (the headline): the leaks do NOT explain the 0.42в†’0.001 collapse вЂ” the bulk is point-in-time SERVING SKEW** (lineup-dependent strong-tier null at morning serve), already on the **Epic 30.3** track. **So construction leakage is now handled (offline numbers + contracts trustworthy); the remaining live-performance lever is serving skew (30.3), not more leak-hunting.** Shipped regression guards: `assert_no_leakage_sequential_posteriors.sql` + `test_seq_asof_guard.py` (prevent recurrence). `ablation_results/feature_leakage_audit.md`.
- **E12 вњ… STRUCTURAL AC MET (2026-06-19) вЂ” serving is sound; the collapse was a benchmark artifact, not a misalignment.** Training + serve read the same table; only `has_full_data` differs в†’ the 0.42в†’0.001 gap is **point-in-time value-completeness** (sparse AM / dense post-backfill), so **0.42 was an optimistic dense re-read.** The fix pre-existed (33.0 pre_lineup tier drops lineup-gated NULL families; 30.3 post_lineup re-score; 30.13 freshness gate). E12 added the **tier-aware parity harness + 21-test standing guard**; live-sparse run в†’ all 3 targets PASS, 0 strong-tier degraded. **Implications:** E1.9 must be **tier-aware** (rebuild/evaluate pre_lineup vs post_lineup separately; don't grade the morning model on dense re-reads); the honest morning target is below 0.42. **Latent risk (only observable live via the standing harness):** a strong-tier feature *inside* the pre_lineup contract arriving all-null some morning = a new serving bug. Remaining: longitudinal live-skill forward-validation (~2вЂ“3 wk).
- **E3.0 вњ…** built + live-validated (2026-06-17) вЂ” `feature_pregame_edge_market`.
- **E3.0b вњ…** built вЂ” bookmaker drift model quantified the decay (soft books' distance to Pinnacle ~halved 2021в†’2025). **Commit the artifacts** (`feature_edge_book_market_era_quality`, `feature_edge_sharp_anchor_backtest`) вЂ” reusable analysis regardless of E4's death.
- **E3.1 рџ”ґ** no-edge (predict-the-move).
- **E4 рџ”ґ CLOSED (2026-06-18)** вЂ” "bet soft toward Pinnacle": a **real, monotone CLV gradient (the program's first non-null signal)** but **too small to beat vig** (~0.5вЂ“0.9 prob-points CLV vs the ~4% soft vig) в†’ **not cashable**; pooled ROI negative, per-season noise, totals same. Killed on **ROI net of vig** (the cashability gate); PBO/DSR not run вЂ” it can't rescue a negative (reserved for *apparent positives*). **The CLV signal still feeds the honest transparency/fair-value app surfaces (E9.11/E9.12) вЂ” just not as "+EV bets."**
- **E13.1 рџ”ґ KILLED (2026-06-21) вЂ” market-anchored residual model fails CLV, both tiers, 8,161 games / 3 purged seasons.** Anchoring to the line + learning the residual is **strictly worse than the market-blind point model** (which is itself the best CLV config at a tiny ~0.2pp вЂ” thinner than E4's dead ~0.5вЂ“0.9pp); DSR excess-over-drift = 0 (doesn't beat always-bet-home). **This is the 4th independent confirmation H2H straight-bet edge is dead (after E3.1, E4, E1.9).** Implication: stop hunting H2H edge; the remaining model-track edge hope narrows to **totals-distribution (E2) + props (E5)** (softer markets), and the H2H model stays live for product value (projections + CLV/fair-value), not "+EV bets." Full detail in the E13 block.
- **E3.3 latency-arbitrage рџ…їпёЏ PARKED** вЂ” the only un-killed E4-adjacent thread, but a **sub-second ops/infra bet incompatible with the manual-advisory model** (a human can't win a seconds race vs a soft book's repricing) and not analyzable on 30-min snapshots. The lead-time/freshness ops work still helps CLV/transparency вЂ” not as a cashable edge.

**Strategic read:** H2H straight-bet edge is closed on **both** heads (E3.1 + E4), and now the program's apparent **#1 model signal (bullpen EB) turned out to be a within-game leak** (E2.1b) вЂ” a sobering but valuable correction that also **names the mechanism for the offlineв†’live collapse** and makes the **de-leak (E1.7) the highest-value model-track item right now** (it may explain why honest live skill has been ~0). **Update (E1.7, 2026-06-18):** de-leaking didn't only subtract вЂ” it **revealed real team-strength signal** (`elo_diff`, `pythagorean_win_exp_diff`) that the leaky bullpen rank had masked in the H2H contracts. That's a modestly hopeful sign: the honest H2H models may carry genuine (if small) fundamentals once the leak is gone вЂ” **but this is unproven until the post-E1.8 retrain + a forward/serving-parity check** (offline importance в‰  live edge; H2H straight-bet edge is still closed on the cashability gate). **Update (E1.8 в†’ E12, 2026-06-18/19) вЂ” the live gap, diagnosed AND structurally handled:** E1.8 found leakage isn't the main driver; the bulk of 0.42в†’0.001 is point-in-time value-completeness at serve. **E12 then resolved it structurally: there's NO train/serve misalignment** вЂ” the fix (33.0 pre_lineup tier + 30.3 post_lineup re-score) was already built, and a tier-aware harness + standing guard now PROVE the served matrix is complete per tier (all 3 targets PASS on a live-sparse day). **Two carry-forwards:** (1) **the 0.42 benchmark is optimistic** (dense re-read) вЂ” the honest morning target is lower; the actionable edge is the post_lineup re-score; (2) **E1.9 must rebuild + evaluate per tier** so it doesn't re-introduce the optimistic trap. Remaining E12 work = longitudinal live-skill forward-validation (~2вЂ“3 wk). Remaining betting-edge hope = **totals-derivatives (E2) + props (E5)**, valued as an honest distribution/derivative *architecture* rather than any single dominant feature. Durable product value = **transparency/CLV surfaces + the fantasy vertical** (which never needed an edge). Reinforces "subscriptions, not betting profit, fund the early days" (`../gtm_strategy.md` В§0).

> **рџ”’ H2H PREDICTION IS A NON-NEGOTIABLE PRODUCT FEATURE (operator 2026-06-21).** Surfacing a calibrated win-probability for every game is **a hard product requirement вЂ” there is no viable product without it.** Two separate objectives, do not conflate: **(A) the PREDICTION** = the honest win-prob we surface, optimized for **accuracy + CALIBRATION (Brier / log-loss / ECE / reliability), NOT CLV** вЂ” alive, central, permanent; **(B) the EDGE** = beating the close / cashability (CLV/ROI) вЂ” *that* is what's dead (E3.1/E4/E1.9/E13.1), and we simply don't claim it. A well-calibrated predictor that can't beat an efficient market is still an excellent product feature; the two aren't in tension. **Honest ceiling:** MLB single-game H2H is inherently high-variance (best team ~60%, worst ~40%) в†’ any calibrated estimate lands near the market's ~55вЂ“58%; the product win is a **trustworthy, well-calibrated, explained** estimate + the "why" (SHAP) + honest variance framing, not superior accuracy or a beat-the-book claim. **v6 (de-leaked + calibrated) IS that honest prediction.** So: the H2H model stays a first-class served model; the model-track H2H goal is **prediction quality (esp. calibration), not edge** вЂ” see E13.6.

---

## рџ”¬ E13 вЂ” Liquid-Market Model Re-Evaluation  *(Session A В· model R&D В· commissioned 2026-06-21)*
**Why now:** E1.9 confirmed the straight H2H/totals point-models are signal-thin on the matrices/architectures we've tried. The operator's call: people pay for these liquid markets, so we owe a *real* edge search before accepting the thin verdict. **Honest base rate:** MLB ML/totals are among the most efficient markets вЂ” durable edge is rare, thin, and decays. So this is a **bounded, kill-gated R&D bet**, run with full LdP discipline (purged CV, **PBO<0.2 + DSR>0**, **forward CLV** the cashability gate), not an open-ended fishing trip. Each workstream gets a **pre-registered hypothesis + kill criterion**; empty stones get killed, not rationalized.

> **рџ§­ STRATEGIC DECISION вЂ” market-aware modeling is now IN SCOPE for E13 (operator 2026-06-21).** The program has been deliberately **market-blind**; that's likely the single biggest reason the edge reads ~0 (predicting games from scratch vs a price that already embeds sharp money). E13 may build **market-AWARE** models. **Honest-framing implication:** a market-aware model's "edge" is the *residual it adds on top of the line* в†’ it must be judged on **forward CLV / beating the close**, not accuracy, and the product story becomes "we find specific spots the market misprices, proven by CLV" (a *stronger*, more defensible narrative than "we predict games") вЂ” but ONLY once it clears forward CLV. Market-blind stays the default for the existing served point-models; market-aware is an E13 R&D exception, gated.

| **E13.8** вњ… | **Market-accuracy benchmark вЂ” yearГ—book line quality (H2H + totals)** | **вњ… DONE 2026-06-23 вЂ” report `ablation_results/e13_8_market_accuracy_benchmark.md` + widened census analysis `dbt/analyses/e13_8_market_accuracy_benchmark.sql` (all ~50 oddsapi books, compile-only / zero warehouse cost).** рџ”‘ **What we're targeting:** (1) **H2H ceiling is thin** вЂ” Pinnacle (в‰€ the low-vig sharps betonlineag/lowvig/onexbet, within noise) closes at **Brier ~0.245**, beating the home-base-rate floor (~0.249) by only **~0.002вЂ“0.005 and not every season** (2023 & partial-2026 sit *at/above* the floor) в†’ corroborates E13.6; **no headroom to beat the close.** (2) **Totals over/under PRICE is a coin flip** вЂ” *every* book incl. Pinnacle at **Brier ~0.250 = no-skill**, over-rate 0.49вЂ“0.51 (lines well-centered); all info is in the **NUMBER** вЂ” line **MAE ~3.4вЂ“3.7 runs / RMSE ~4.5**, irreducibly noisy, no book sharper than another beyond noise. | **E13.9** рџ†• | **Selective "best-bet" model вЂ” abstention + betting-utility objective on the SOFT markets** | **NEW (operator 2026-06-23) вЂ” the "discriminate on the BEST bets, don't grade on predicting every game" idea.** Complement to E13.4: E13.4 = alpha-from-FEATURES; Built `betting_ml/utils/derivative_eval.py` (pure: F5/NRFI settlement, 2/3-way de-vig, Brier+calibration-z, static ROI net of vig, OLS mechanical-derivation, BH-FDR) + `betting_ml/scripts/derivative_eval/eval_derivatives.py` (reads E5.1 `mlb/props/` в†’ settles from `stg_batter_pitches` в†’ bridge в†’ `mart_closing_line_value` в†’ dossier; `--smoke`) + 21 tests (fast gate 831вњ…) + pre-registration. Dossier `ablation_results/e13_13_*` committed. **Caveat for any E2.6 follow-on:** F5 settlement doesn't yet exclude rain-shortened/<5-inning VOID games. _(orig в†“)_ **NEW (operator 2026-06-23, from "The Logic of Sports Betting").** Operationalizes the E2.6 derivative gate now that the F5/NRFI/team-total/alt odds are backfilled (correct `*_1st_N_innings` keys). **THESIS (Miller-Davidow + E13.8): market-makers price FEATURED markets tight but DERIVATIVES loose (lower limits/effort) в†’ the main line is efficient (E13.8) but the lazier derivatives may not be.** Four angles: **(1) extend the E13.8 benchmark to derivatives** вЂ” per-book per-derivative efficiency (closing Brier / line-MAE vs the realized derivative outcome, SETTLED from our pitch data: first-5 runs, 1st-inning runs) в†’ find the least-efficient markets + soft-book spread + the (higher) derivative VIG; **(2) mechanical-derivation check** вЂ” do books derive F5/team-total/alt by a fixed rule off the main line? where the TRUE relationship deviates (e.g. ace-driven F5 suppression > the generic fraction) = the exploit; **(3) model-vs-market gate (E2.6)** вЂ” the E13.2 PA-sim / E2.3 distribution gives native derivative distributions в†’ gate each vs its OWN close, **PBO<0.2 + DSR>0 + FORWARD CLV**; **(4) retail-bias** вЂ” directional over/favorite shading at soft books = a side to fade. **рџ”’ HONEST BAR (Miller-Davidow's own discipline): CLV is the measure; softer в‰  free вЂ” derivatives carry HIGHER VIG + LOWER LIMITS, so the edge must be forward-CLV-positive NET OF THE DERIVATIVE'S OWN VIG, not just statistically present.** Needs: derivative odds (backfilling now) + outcomes (our pitch data) + a model distribution (E13.2 sim or E2.3). **рџџў DATA UPGRADE 2026-06-24 (E2.0b-fix): LIVE forward F5/NRFI capture is now ON** вЂ” the cron was fixed to the correct `*_1st_5_innings` keys (16 books live: FanDuel/BetMGM/Pinnacle/Bovada/DraftKings/Caesars/вЂ¦) + deployed; the earlier "F5 not offered live / backtest-only" belief was a wrong-key artifact across THREE probes. в‡’ E13.13 now has BOTH the historical backfill (train/backtest) AND a live forward F5-close feed в†’ its **FORWARD-CLV leg can accrue PROSPECTIVELY on real captured closes** (the cleanest CLV test, not a retrospective proxy). Cross-ref E2.6 / E13.8 / E3.0b / E13.2 / E2.0b-fix. | a derivative clears forward-CLV-positive net of vig @ PBO<0.2/DSR>0 в†’ ship; else trustworthy null в†’ dossier (+ closes the betting-edge thesis after the efficient main line в†’ product-quality + fantasy stands). |

**Priority (REVISED 2026-06-21 after E13.1 kill):** **E13.0 вњ… HOLD В· E13.1 рџ”ґ KILLED.** The two highest-leverage H2H *edge* bets came back empty в†’ **H2H straight-bet EDGE is DONE; stop hunting it.** **BUT the H2H *prediction* is a non-negotiable product feature (see the рџ”’ decision above) в†’ E13.6 (calibration/prediction-quality) is now a standing model-track priority, judged on Brier/ECE not CLV.** Remaining *edge* search **pivots to TOTALS + props** (softer markets), not more H2H edge: **(1) E13.3** next вЂ” sub-models on clean data (operator's hypothesis; cheap, run to closure, LOW expectations + firm kill); **(2) pull E2.2/E2.3 forward** (the per-side totals *distribution* вЂ” the strategic read's actual named edge hope); **(3) E13.2** only as a **totals-distribution engine feeding E2** (not an ML-edge hunt); **(4) E13.4** scoped to **totals/run-environment signals** (team defense OAA/DRS, bullpen availability, weatherГ—park) where there's unexplored structure. **E13.5 deprioritized** вЂ” its main consumer (E13.1 forward CLV) is dead; only revive for a totals/props challenger worth shadow-serving. **Strategic frame:** `best_alpha = 0` is now strongly evidenced on H2H from 4 angles вЂ” "delivering on liquid markets" = best-in-class honest projections + transparency/CLV (the GTM wedge), NOT a demonstrated ML edge. ~~The only live betting-edge hope narrows to totals-distribution (E2) + props (E5).~~ **рџЏЃ EDGE SEARCH EXHAUSTED вЂ” UPDATED 2026-06-30:** those last hopes are now CLOSED too вЂ” **E5.4 (K-props) NULL + E13.13 (derivatives) NULL**, on top of H2H Г—5, main total coin-flip (E13.8), and 6 model-track nulls (E13.2/2b/3/4/10 + PA-vs-log5). **No cashable PRE-GAME edge survives honest validation in any MLB liquid market tested.** в‡’ Treat "find an MLB pre-game edge" as CLOSED; concentrate model effort on the PRODUCT (calibrated projections E2.3/E5.2, transparency E13.6/E13.10, CLV-tracking) + the FANTASY vertical (E7/E8 вЂ” projection quality IS the product, no market-efficiency wall). **The only UNTESTED edge hypotheses left (all lower-priority than the product): (1) E2.6 forward-CLV on live captured closes (low prior, empty offline target list); (2) MULTI-SPORT / college markets (untested вЂ” plausibly softer than MLB; the fall push); (3) live/in-game markets (untested вЂ” different infra); (4) ~~CROSS-MARKET RELATIVE VALUE~~ вњ… **TESTED в†’ NULL (E13.14, 2026-06-30): the constellation is internally COHERENT too** вЂ” `info_gain<0` on all 3 relations (the books' posted lines beat their own cross-market implied quantities, every time), PBO 0.487, negative control validated. The "different mechanism" came back efficient as well.** рџ†• **SPEC'D 2026-06-30 (operator-requested edge re-examination):** **E13.14** (cross-market RV probe вЂ” the new mechanism; tests propsв†”team-total / team-totalв†”game-total / sidesв†”totals, F5в†”main = negative control; Bayesian high-credence-inconsistency selection) В· **E13.15** (in-game/live-line probe-FIRST вЂ” historical-in-play availability + the Bayesian live-update thesis) В· вЏ° **a pre-turnover DATA-GRAB** (`team_totals`+`alt_totals`+`spreads` before the Odds API 5Mв†’100K drop ~7/17 вЂ” E13.14's top relations are BLOCKED on `team_totals` not being in S3). вљ пёЏ honest prior on all four = guarded, but each tests a mechanism the nulls did NOT cover. вљ пёЏ **the 2-week-to-ASB pressure must NOT relax the gate вЂ” E5.4 + E13.13 EACH caught a tempting false-positive; a shipped mirage is worse than no edge.** This does NOT change the business: subscriptions fund it, the GTM wedge was always honest analytics, not a tipping edge (`../gtm_strategy.md` В§0). The discipline is WORKING вЂ” E5.4 and E13.13 each CAUGHT a tempting false-positive and killed it; shipping a data-mined mirage to paying users would be the real failure.

The Delta WRITE path = delta-rs (`deltalake` / `pl.write_delta`) вЂ” a new box dep. вњ… Delta STILL HOLDS: the "DuckDB writes it natively" point was misattributed (Iceberg's); the DECIDING reasons вЂ” catalog-optional + Polars-native pairing + we don't need Snowflake to read the lakehouse вЂ” stand; delta-rs is a mature catalog-optional writer. Reconsider ONLY if SF-reads-the-lakehouse or a 2nd engine (Spark/Trino) becomes real (neither is planned).** рџђ»вЂЌвќ„пёЏ **DATAFRAME = Polars** вЂ” Arrow-native, so Deltaв†’Polarsв†’DuckDB is zero-copy (pandas forces conversions); Polars reads/writes Delta natively (`pl.read_delta`/`write_delta`). вљ пёЏ **SCOPING (don't big-bang it): adopt Polars for NEW code + the Delta read/serve HOT paths first; convert the ~180 offline training scripts opportunistically, NOT in one rewrite.** рџ”ґ **MODEL-I/O GOTCHA: trained sklearn models expect pandas DataFrames (feature names/dtypes/order) вЂ” keep a clean Polarsв†’pandas conversion at the MODEL boundary (or retrain on the new pipeline); ties to the existing sklearn-version-pin follow-up.** рџЋЇ **No longer a maybe: the migration's repeated SILENT-corruption fragility (INC-17-P2 / woba-zero / INC-19 type-drift / INC-20 OOM / INC-21 / INC-22) is the reason вЂ” raw Parquet has no schema-evolution, no ACID, no retention/compaction, no point-in-time, so we keep curing these by hand. A table format retires those CLASSES structurally.** SEQUENCING: ship the migration (W8aв†’W8b) в†’ run **E11.22** (the feature-serving integrity audit) в†’ its findings = the evidence base + the table-by-table priority list в†’ then START E11.20 (no longer "after the break / if cost-justified" вЂ” it's the committed on-ramp to multi-sport, since the layout chosen here is replicated Г—3 sports). The Delta-vs-Iceberg + scope detail below still stands. WHY now-plausible: as of 2026 DuckDB has real WRITE support for both вЂ” **Iceberg** (1.4 LTS Sept-2025; v1.5.3 May-2026 added `MERGE INTO`/`ALTER TABLE`/partition transforms вЂ” but writes REQUIRE an attached REST catalog = new infra) and **Delta** (full write v1.5.0, GA v1.5.2; **catalog-OPTIONAL** вЂ” just a `_delta_log` on the S3 path). So a table format is now writable FROM our DuckDB stack, not just readable. WHY it's attractive for US specifically: it retires two recurring incident CLASSES structurally вЂ” **INC-19 (NUMBERв†”FLOAT drift в†’ DROP+rebuild) becomes managed schema-evolution (`ALTER TABLE`)**, and **INC-20 (unbounded daily-re-export partitions в†’ OOM) becomes snapshot-expiration + compaction + overwrite-in-place** вЂ” plus ACID commits and в­ђ **time-travel / point-in-time queries** (a real leakage-audit + backtest-reproducibility asset for a betting model: "what did the feature store look like as of date X"). WHY WAIT (don't do mid-migration): (1) stacking a format conversion on top of the unfinished Parquet migration turns one mess into two вЂ” finish Parquet + the INC-19/20 hardening + stabilize FIRST; (2) the single biggest Iceberg-specific win (ONE table both DuckDB AND Snowflake read natively в†’ collapses the dual-branch `lakehouse_ext`+parity+refresh machinery) is being MOOTED by our own Cortex-only roadmap, which removes the Snowflake feature build / dual-branch anyway в†’ in the DuckDB-only end-state the cross-engine benefit shrinks. FORMAT CHOICE: вњ… **RESOLVED 2026-06-29 = Delta Lake on-path, RE-VALIDATED by E11.20a 2026-07-02.** Dataframe layer = **Polars** (Arrow-native; pairs with Delta + DuckDB zero-copy). **вњ… JUSTIFICATION (E11.20a): the incident-class retirement вЂ” INC-19 (additive schema-evolution, though a genuine stored NUMBERв†”FLOAT flip still needs deliberate migration, NOT free) + INC-20 (compaction/vacuum) + time-travel (leakage-audit/backtest reproducibility) вЂ” is SUFFICIENT to justify E11.20 on its own; the MERGE-into-partition win (the 40-min-job cure) is a ROLLOUT AC to QUANTIFY on real box-scale history (the POC couldn't at 1.5M rows local), NOT a go/no-go gate.** рџ§Ё ROLLOUT must design around the E11.20a gotchas (full list in `docs/e11_20a_delta_polars_spike.md`): delta-rs WRITE path (not DuckDB) + bake `deltalake`/`polars`/DuckDB-`delta`-ext into the arm64 box image; vacuum(0) DESTROYS time-travel в†’ keep 168h retention (the vacuumв†”time-travel tension); PIN `deltalake==1.6.x` (1.x API churn); MERGEв†’scheduled `optimize.compact()` companion (MERGE makes small files); partition-aware MERGE predicate (else forfeits the O(partition) win); SF-ext-over-Delta carries the W8a binary-ts risk в†’ prefer NO Snowflake read of Delta; delta-rs S3 writes must use the instance role (the AKID landmine, new surface); `pl.scan_delta` (lazy) not `read_delta` for mart-sized. SCOPE (when pulled): convert ONE table family (e.g. `feature_pregame_*`) to Delta-on-path, measure schema-evolution + retention + time-travel ergonomics vs the Parquet+cast+guard baseline. вЏ­пёЏ **TRIGGERS to pull forward:** schema-drift toil keeps recurring DESPITE the INC-19 cast+guard В· we want point-in-time backtest reproducibility В· we add a 2nd compute engine. (Sources captured 2026-06-29: DuckDB Iceberg-writes + Delta-extension docs.)

## рџ’° Cost watch (baseline 2026-06)
вњ… **UPDATED 2026-07-02 вЂ” the cost picture has TRANSFORMED (INC-16 closed + the decommission):** **Dagster+ (~$275вЂ“325/mo) + Railway (~$12/mo) = $0 (accounts closed).** Cost centers now: **AWS ~$73/mo** (the r6g.large box + EIP + S3/DynamoDB/Lambda serverless-negligible) В· **Snowflake вЂ” minimal, still ~$8/day during the DUAL-WRITE window, drops sharply once the cutover flips complete** (Cortex + state tables stay) В· **subscriptions** (Claude Code, The Odds API, FanGraphs). в‡’ from the ~$500вЂ“620/mo baseline below to roughly **~$73 AWS + shrinking-Snowflake + subs** вЂ” the Dagster+ elimination alone banked the single biggest cut, now REALIZED. _(historical 2026-06 baseline в†“)_
Pre-revenue monthly burn (~$500вЂ“620/mo total), with the target obvious:
- **Snowflake вЂ” ~$287 в†’ trending ~$359/mo (+25% MoM); ~60% of spend, GROWING. THE target.** (Last month $287.40; MTD 6/18 $225.90.) **рџљЁ 6/22 AUDIT BOMBSHELL вЂ” the cost-opt was aimed at the wrong target: 96.7% of Snowflake credits are UNTAGGED.** Last-7-day run = **23.35 credits total; 22.58 (96.7%, 89,210 queries) UNTAGGED**; every E11.3-tagged job (all dbt builds + dagster jobs + crons) = **3.3% (~0.77 cr).** в‡’ the heavy Statcast dbt marts (W1's target) are tagged-and-TINY (~0.02вЂ“0.04 cr/run, once-daily incremental) в†’ **W1 will NOT meaningfully cut credits.** **QUERY_HISTORY drill-down (6/22) identified it:** the "untagged" set is the **normal dbt/pipeline workload (`DBT_RW`/`COMPUTE_WH`) that isn't carrying QUERY_TAG** вЂ” `dbt_version: 2.0.0` = **dbt-fusion в†’ E11.3's tag hook doesn't propagate to per-model queries** (not a hidden poll). **Real drivers: в­ђ `feature_pregame` CTAS rebuilt 1,861Г—/7d (~266/day) = #1; `ALTER ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS` Г—8,850 (DDL on every write); dead Parlay inserts (~3,570, self-resolving post-decommission); a small app-backend Snowflake read path.** **в†’ #1 cost action = E11.9: fix dbt-fusion tagging + cut the intraday `feature_pregame` rebuild frequency + the ADD-COLUMN-per-write waste + auto-suspend COMPUTE_WH.** W1 deprioritized as a COST lever (it's the rebuild FREQUENCY, not the marts).
- **Dagster вЂ” рџљЁ UP, not down: $36.20 since 6/18 (~$8/day в‰€ ~$240/mo), ABOVE the old $50вЂ“100 estimate despite E11.4 removing ~47.6% of run-MINUTES.** Why the minute-cut didn't cut the bill: E11.4 removed the *light* polling schedules, but the cost is dominated by **long-wall-clock dbt rebuilds metered via blocking-poll (the E11.0b gap)** вЂ” a Dagster op that triggers the runner + polls `/status` stays metered for the full dbt run. The Snowflake audit showed **`feature_pregame` rebuilds ~266Г—/day** в†’ each metered on Dagster too (same root cause, two invoices). **And W1 just ADDED Dagster compute** вЂ” the `ingest_statcast_to_s3_op`/`run_w1_lakehouse_op` dead-end tail runs the DuckDB build *inside Dagster* (parallel window = paying for DuckDB build + Snowflake build). **в†’ Fix: E11.9 #1 (cut the feature_pregame rebuild frequency) cuts BOTH bills; RE-ELEVATE E11.0b (blocking-poll metering, now a big chunk); move the W1 DuckDB build to a Railway CRON (E11.4 pattern), not a Dagster op.** В§6 principle holds: Dagster *coordinates*, Railway/DuckDB *executes* вЂ” heavy compute on the Dagster meter is the suspect.
- **Odds API $119/mo** вЂ” ~~consolidation candidate: SportsGameOdds~~ **KEEP (operator 2026-06-23): F5 IS available from The Odds API (`*_1st_5_innings` keys) в†’ the SportsGameOdds-for-F5 swap rationale is gone; stay on the incumbent. Only revisit if F5 BOOK coverage proves too thin. вЂ” see E2.0c.**
- Vercel $30 В· Railway ~$12 В· **AWS ~$2вЂ“3/mo (negligible вЂ” MTD $1.34; serverless stack basically free at beta scale).**
- **Railway plan = Hobby ($5/mo, incl. $5 usage); sufficient at beta scale.** Compute is NOT the constraint (Hobby includes up to 48 vCPU/48 GB per service, 8/8 per replica вЂ” the always-on dbt-runner + DuckDB Statcast transforms fit). Below $20 usage, Hobby is cheaper; current ~$12 в†’ stay on Hobby for now. (Per-service resource ceilings are the same on both tiers, so the upgrade is about credits/features, not capacity.)
- **рџџў Cost-opt ACTIVATED NOW (operator 2026-06-18) вЂ” "keep Snowflake at minimum until profitable."** E11 is **no longer parked**. **Done this wave:** E11.3 (tagging) вњ…, E11.0 (dbt-runner substrate) вњ…, E11.4 (intradayв†’crons, ~47.6% Dagster run-min off-meter) вњ…, **E11.5 (engine decision: stay fusion) вњ…**, **E11.2-T2 (state-aware daily builds) вњ… LIVE 6/19** (the dbt-fusion "wall" was just a YAML format issue вЂ” `config:`-nest freshness вЂ” fixed in E11.5; dbt-runner redeployed). **Next:** **E11.1-W1 (heavy Statcast marts в†’ dbt-duckdb/S3)** = the PRIMARY remaining structural Snowflake lever (unblocked, runs on fusion); then E11.0b (residual Dagster dbt) + E11.6 (Parlay cleanup, low). вљ пёЏ **6/22 AUDIT вЂ” HONEST EXPECTATION (operator confirmed the intuition 2026-06-22): Dagster DOWN, Snowflake FLAT-to-slightly-UP.** Why: the only real Snowflake lever (**A2.15 = E11.1-W1**) is in its **parallel-validation window вЂ” marts NOT decommissioned, so the S3/DuckDB path runs ALONGSIDE the live Snowflake builds (double-run, possibly +Snowflake this week)**; T2's daily-skip savings are unverified + small; everything else shipped (E11.4 etc.) cut **Dagster**, not Snowflake. So **the 6/22 audit = "Dagster win banked (E11.4) + W1 not yet realized," NOT the Snowflake measurement.** **рџЋЇ The REAL Snowflake checkpoint is AFTER the W1 decommission (~6/26+):** once parity passes 6/25 в†’ external tables в†’ drop the Snowflake `mart_pitch_*` builds в†’ re-run the audit; THAT is when credits should fall. **Run the 6/22 audit:** `uv run python scripts/ops/snowflake_cost_by_job.py --days 7` (credit-by-job via the E11.3 QUERY_TAG) + the Dagster+ usage CSV, vs the 6/18 baseline. _(Master-guide reconciliation: A2.15 lakehouse = E11.1-W1 [parallel window]; A2.16 Dagster-compute-reduction = delivered via E11.4 [schedules removed]; 30.3 = E12 вњ…; 12.10вЂІ Pinnacle sharp-money = вќЊ no-edge, +0.0095 vs +0.01 gate; 12.3.5 вњ… done, residual uk/au region-widen budget-gated.)_ Cost-opt also unlocks the F5 (E2.0c) budget.
